VETERANS HEALTHCARE



How long are VA wait times? Use simulations to see the distribution of possibilities.



    Applet by   Skew The Script (authors: Max Cembalest and Dashiell Young-Saver)
    Applet inspired by   this sampling distribution applet   (by David Lane & fellow contributors)
    Background image by University of Michigan Health Lab.




\begin{align} \bar{x} \sim Norm ( \mu_{\bar{x}} = \mu, \sigma_{\bar{x}} = \frac{\sigma}{\sqrt{n}}) \end{align}
